- `L1809` The file sometimes treats semantic thickness as something fully supplied by the author.  _(TENSIONS_CONTRADICTIONS/item_06; ai-prompting-and-description.md:L19134)_
- `L1810` Calling a description “operative” because it can regenerate an artifact is insufficient.  _(TENSIONS_CONTRADICTIONS/item_07; ai-prompting-and-description.md:L19138)_
- `L1811` The movement from image generation to world modeling is asserted too quickly.  _(TENSIONS_CONTRADICTIONS/item_08; ai-prompting-and-description.md:L19142)_
- `L1812` The file defines imagetext too smoothly as a fused mixed representation.  _(TENSIONS_CONTRADICTIONS/item_01; ai-prompting-and-description.md:L19465)_
- `L1813` The draft sometimes moves from “all media are mixed” to “text and image are two decodings of one latent representation.” The first is a media-theoretical claim; the second is an architectural claim that does not hold uniformly across multimodal systems.  _(TENSIONS_CONTRADICTIONS/item_02; ai-prompting-and-description.md:L19469)_
- `L1814` Calling the embedding itself the imagetext risks relocating the concept into an inaccessible technical interior.  _(TENSIONS_CONTRADICTIONS/item_03; ai-prompting-and-description.md:L19473)_
- `L1815` The text’s formal analogy- <image : image model :: world : world model> -is cleaner than- <image : image model :: video : world model>, but it remains asymmetrical.  _(TENSIONS_CONTRADICTIONS/item_04; ai-prompting-and-description.md:L19477)_
- `L1816` The definition of video model as predicting visible continuation remains too narrow for modern systems that accept camera motion, image conditions, edits, or actions.  _(TENSIONS_CONTRADICTIONS/item_05; ai-prompting-and-description.md:L19489)_
- `L1817` The file gives action conditioning special status, but action conditioning alone is insufficient.  _(TENSIONS_CONTRADICTIONS/item_06; ai-prompting-and-description.md:L19493)_
- `L1818` The proposed world-text is introduced before its relation to prompt, scene graph, program, simulation script, game state, and world specification is clarified.  _(TENSIONS_CONTRADICTIONS/item_07; ai-prompting-and-description.md:L19497)_
- `L1819` The Axis Inverter draft correctly criticizes visual coherence as false evidence of simulation, but it still treats “physics” as the principal missing criterion.  _(TENSIONS_CONTRADICTIONS/item_08; ai-prompting-and-description.md:L19501)_
- `L1820` The file oscillates between descriptive taxonomy and normative argument.  _(TENSIONS_CONTRADICTIONS/item_09; ai-prompting-and-description.md:L19505)_
- `L1821` The distinction between video model and world model is necessary, but the draft makes it too absolute.  _(TENSIONS_CONTRADICTIONS/item_01; ai-prompting-and-description.md:L19847)_
- `L1822` Action conditioning is treated as the decisive criterion, although it is only a minimum condition.  _(TENSIONS_CONTRADICTIONS/item_02; ai-prompting-and-description.md:L19851)_
- `L1823` The phrase “a world model must explain what changes” overstates the requirement.  _(TENSIONS_CONTRADICTIONS/item_03; ai-prompting-and-description.md:L19855)_
- `L1824` The proposed extension from imagetext to worldtext is not structurally automatic.  _(TENSIONS_CONTRADICTIONS/item_04; ai-prompting-and-description.md:L19859)_
- `L1825` Defining a world principally through state, actions, and transitions imports a Markov-decision-process ontology.  _(TENSIONS_CONTRADICTIONS/item_05; ai-prompting-and-description.md:L19863)_
- `L1826` The draft privileges physics as the test of worldhood.  _(TENSIONS_CONTRADICTIONS/item_06; ai-prompting-and-description.md:L19867)_
- `L1827` The analogy “image model renders appearance” understates what image models can encode and overstates the stability of “appearance” as a category.  _(TENSIONS_CONTRADICTIONS/item_07; ai-prompting-and-description.md:L19871)_
- `L1828` The proposed worldtext risks duplicating existing concepts such as scene graph, game state, simulation script, knowledge graph, interactive fiction, executable specification, or digital twin unless its unique relation among these is made explicit.  _(TENSIONS_CONTRADICTIONS/item_08; ai-prompting-and-description.md:L19875)_
